French Municipal Council 100

,

Attention to Sanitation within the Concession

Advising Land Owners to Enclose Vacant Lots with Fences

The French Municipal Council has always paid attention to sanitation within the concession. Now that the Shanghai Incident has passed and summer is approaching, it has issued a special notice to all business owners, asking them to assist the council in maintaining sanitation within the concession. The notice reads: "Regarding the matter of sanitation, the difficulties encountered by this council in maintaining health and sanitation within the concession may not be fully understood by the general public. In fact, this council is constantly striving for this goal. It has been found that the most important task for this council is to maintain the cleanliness of the numerous vacant lots within the new concession, as these vacant lots easily become breeding grounds for filth. Therefore, various departments of this council have repeatedly instructed people to enclose these vacant lots with fences. However, in practice, this has been very difficult, as there are many obstacles hindering progress. In some cases, the owners of the vacant lots often avoid meeting with us. In other cases, those who are contacted are merely tenants, and these tenants all make excuses, claiming that the real owners should be responsible for enclosing the vacant lots with fences, and they refuse the council's requests. This results in futile back-and-forth correspondence with little success. Sometimes, the vacant lots are jointly owned by three or four owners, and these owners have differing opinions and do not respond to the council's letters. Therefore, the biggest obstacle encountered by this council is the excessive disregard of the owners of vacant lots for issues related to public health. They are unable or unwilling to understand that enclosing the vacant lots, while being their duty, is also in their own interest. However, despite these many difficulties, this council has been able to achieve commendable success. By the end of 1931, only a few vacant lots in this concession remained unenclosed. Unfortunately, in the past year and a half, the council's work of the past three years has been almost completely destroyed. This is because various departments of this council are currently focusing on defense work, and as a result, the monitoring efforts have not been comprehensive, leading to the complete disappearance of these fences when refugees flooded the concession. Now, this fencing work will continue, as such work is urgently needed at a time when general health conditions are poor and summer is approaching. However, in order to quickly achieve our goals, the cooperation of all landowners with this council is essential. This council sincerely hopes that all landowners will understand that enclosing vacant lots, while being in the public interest, is also in their own personal interest, as this type of fencing is indeed the most effective guarantee against others dumping garbage on their vacant lots, as well as digging soil, and other various acts of theft. In order to prevent people from using this bamboo as fuel, this council intends to use tarred bamboo as fencing material, so that the odor emitted when the bamboo is burned may prevent many people from using it for cooking. As for the council's supervision work, it should also be strengthened, and offenders should be severely punished as a warning to others. Furthermore, this council also hopes that all residents will pay attention and not pile garbage on roads or vacant lots, and that garbage bins should be placed according to regulations and moved to the side of the road when garbage trucks pass by for easy removal. In addition, there are many residents who do not supervise their servants when they dump garbage, and then turn around and criticize this council. In fact, such criticism should be directed at them. Therefore, this council believes that regarding the issue of improving health and cleanliness, if all residents do not understand the importance of public cooperation, then even the efforts of this council will be in vain. However, we hope that as long as we raise the awareness of the Chinese and foreign residents in the concession about the need for public cooperation, we can be sure of rapid improvement, which would be fortunate."

The Organization of the Women's Livelihood Cooperative 101

The women's circles in Shanghai, in view of the large number of unemployed female workers due to the recent Shanghai war, which has greatly affected the society's livelihood, have specially founded a Women's Livelihood Cooperative at the end of Hongqing Lane on Xinza Road. The content of its organization is very detailed. A sewing department has now been established, specializing in making Chinese and Western clothing, commercial banners, and daily household items. Because of the low labor costs and exquisite craftsmanship, it is quite popular in society, and the cooperative's business is exceptionally developed. The current president is Ms. Luo Zhi.

Page 8

In order to expand, the cooperative is recruiting members, enrolling students, and hiring Chinese and Western technicians to teach machine sewing skills to cultivate a large number of ladies to meet the urgent needs. Its regulations will be sent upon request by letter.

News from Various Schools 102

Practical Night School The Shanghai Practical Vocational Supplementary Night School, in view of the importance of providing relief to unemployed youth after the war, has already opened a course in engineering drawing, with departments in architectural drawing, mechanical drawing, and surveying and mapping. It is the first vocational supplementary night school of its kind in the country. The course now employs over ten experts, including Mr. Huang Ri, an architect from the Shanghai Hexing Company, and Professor Wang Qin of the Civil Engineering Department of Daxia University. Currently, the number of students enrolled in the architectural drawing department, both face-to-face and correspondence courses, is already in the hundreds, and it is extremely developed. The graduation period is not long, the tuition is low, and the results are significant. Those who are concerned about their own careers after the war can contact Mr. Gan Chunquan, the principal of the school, at the Shanghai Vocational Guidance Center at No. 80 Hualong Road, Shanghai.

Yucai Public School The Shanghai Municipal Council Yucai Public School on Shanhai Pass Road, originally scheduled to hold its sports meet on the 22nd of this month, postponed it to the 29th due to rain. Now, due to continuous rain and the muddy sports field, which is unsuitable for sports, it has been postponed again to the 6th of next month.

News from Various Native Place Associations 103

Guangdong The number of Guangdong people living in Shanghai is approximately 300,000. The most prominent among their organizations are the Guangzhao Public Association, the Guangdong Overseas Chinese Business Federation, and the Chaozhou Native Place Association. However, these are all limited to local affairs and the business community. It can be said that there is no organization that represents all districts and sectors of the province. After the outbreak of the war in northern Shanghai, some Guangdong people organized the Guangdong Native Place Relief Association, which specialized in relief and comfort activities. However, it was later disbanded due to certain circumstances. In February, Guangdong people Wen Zongyao, Feng Shaoshan, Wu Tiecheng, Ma Chaojun, Chen Fumu, Zheng Hongnian, Mai Chaochu, Gao Guangjing, and others gathered various Guangdong organizations and people from all walks of life in Shanghai to initiate a unified Guangdong Native Place Association. After preparations up to now, it has been filed with the Municipal Party Headquarters and the Social Affairs Bureau, becoming a legal organization. The registration of members of the association is also extremely enthusiastic. Its organizational method is quite special, as it is difficult to convene a general meeting of all members due to the large number of people. Therefore, every 200 people form a branch association, and the branch association representatives organize the executive body, which should be the executive committee. Currently, the elected executive committee members include Gao Chengyuan, Fang Diffei, Yuan Liangzou, Zhu Yecang, Lin Junxian, Xia Shiqing, Huo Shi, Liu Zichong, Chen Yien, Chen Yinong, Fu Shunan, Tang Diffei, etc. The inaugural meeting will be held today at the China Society on Weihaiwei Road, and the executive committee members will also take office at the same time.

Kunshan The Kunshan Native Place Association in Shanghai, because farmers in the area previously used grain as collateral to the Farmers Bank to redeem it, encountered war, and the bank, fearing that the collateral would be unsecured, sold all the pledged rice. Now, at this time of year when the new crop is not yet available, farmers have funds to redeem the rice, but the rice is not available, which has a significant impact. Therefore, the association urgently telegraphed the provincial and county governments and the county security committee, requesting that the bank be ordered to quickly use the proceeds from the sale of the pledged rice to purchase rice for redemption in order to maintain the people's food supply.

Love Triangle Struggle 104

Shooting at the Far East Hotel

The Trouble Caused by Lao Ba of Yanchun Lou

Gao Liansheng Gathered a Crowd and Fired Six Shots

Qi Laohu Wounded But Not Killed

This Kind of Spirit Should Go to the Front Lines

At 9:20 PM on March 20th of this year, a brawl occurred in the billiard room of the Far East Hotel on Xizang Road due to a love triangle. At the time, Qi Laohu was shot in six places and was sent to Renji Hospital by his companions. The case was reported to the Old Zha Gate Police Station for the arrest of the criminals. Until the previous day, after Qi Laohu learned that Yang Jian (also known as Xiao Bao or Xiao Yang), a Ningbo native who was present at the shooting, was about to escape to Hankou on the Jiangxin steamer, he reported it to the police station. Detective Feng Xiushan, together with detectives from the French Police Station, went to the Jiangxin steamer at the Sixteen Pu Wharf, arrested Yang, and brought him back to the police station. Yesterday morning, he was escorted to the First Special District Court's Criminal Division One, where Judge Zhou Hanting took the stand for interrogation. The police station's lawyer, Qian Xunjiu, stated that the police station was now prosecuting the defendant based on Article 282, Paragraph 2 of the Criminal Law for attempted murder. It was found that this case occurred on the night of March 20th, when the fugitives Gao Liansheng, Wu Jiming, Xiao Suzhou, etc., went to the billiard room of the Far East Hotel, dragged Qi Laohu into the kitchen, and fired six shots from their guns, causing Qi to be hit by six bullets and fall to the ground. Qi's friend Gao Derong sent him to Renji Hospital and reported it to the police station. At that time, the police station immediately sent detectives to investigate. However, Qi was unwilling to reveal the truth. The next day, Qi was transferred to Baolong Hospital for treatment. Fortunately, the injuries were minor, and he was discharged from the hospital after more than ten days of treatment. Meanwhile, Detective You A'gen learned that the cause of the incident was that Qi Laohu and Gao Liansheng were both in love with Lao Ba, a prostitute at No. 304 Huile Lane, and therefore, a love rivalry arose. When the police station went to Huile Lane to investigate, Lao Ba had moved to the French Concession for business. However, the victim in this case, Qi Laohu, is also an undesirable element in the jurisdiction of the Huishi Police Station. His father used to be Chinese Police Officer No. 415 in the police station. Therefore, when the detectives investigated Qi, he was unwilling to tell the truth. It was not until yesterday that Qi reported to the police station that Yang Jian, who was related to the shooting, was currently on the Jiangxin steamer, intending to escape to Hankou. The police station then arrested Yang. It was found that Yang was Gao Liansheng's follower, etc. According to Qi Laohu, he was related to Gao Liansheng. Gao's original name was Zhu Nansheng, and he was intimate with Yan Chun Lou's Lao Ba, a prostitute in Qunyufang. I didn't know about it at first, so I called for Lao Ba. Later, Gao stated to me that Lao Ba was his lover and asked me not to call for her again. I agreed. Until the night of March 20th, I was playing billiards with my friend Gao Derong at the Far East Hotel when I met Gao Liansheng, who asked me to talk. I went with him, and as soon as I got to the elevator, I saw the defendant and Wu Jiming each pull out a gun and fire six shots at me. I was injured and fell in the kitchen, etc. When questioned, the defendant Yang Jian confessed that on that day, Gao Liansheng gave me an ax and told me to go to the Far East to fight. I didn't know who I was going to fight, so I went with him. I saw that Gao had a gun. When we got to the Far East, I saw Gao call Qi Laohu away. Because I knew Qi, I didn't do anything and slipped out through the back door. Afterwards, Gao told me that because Qi had taken his mistress Lao Ba and often went out to rent rooms, he wanted to kill him. At that time, Gao gave me fifteen yuan to escape to the countryside, and Gao also escaped to Hankou. The previous day, Gao sent me a letter telling me to go to Hankou, so I was arrested on the Jiangxin steamer, etc. After Judge Zhou Hanting verified the facts, he ordered the defendant to be detained and interrogated again next Tuesday.

Qi Rengxi and 105

Zhang Meili's Lawsuit

Qi Sues Requesting Severance of Family Ties

Zhang Countersues Seeking Reimbursement of Living Expenses for Children, Etc.

Qi Rengxi, a politician from Ningbo who once founded the Guanhai Evening News, is currently 44 years old and resides at No. 72 Wanyi Lane, Luban Road, French Concession. He married Zhang Meifeng, also from Ningbo. In the tenth year of the Republic, when Qi was living in Tianjin, Meifeng fell ill. Her younger sister, Zhang Meili (currently 35 years old), went to Tianjin to take care of her sister and developed feelings for Qi. At that time, Qi requested that if his wife died, he would marry Meili as his successor. As a result, their love deepened day by day. Later, Qi's Xiehe Trading Company in Tianjin went bankrupt, and a lawsuit ensued. Meili spent a large sum of money to help Qi resolve the lawsuit. From then on, the two began to live together. Meifeng's illness gradually healed. Qi had told Meili that he was willing to divorce Meifeng and then formally marry her. However, he vaguely delayed it and did not carry it out. Nevertheless, they have been living together ever since and have had seven children. Last year, when Qi moved to Shanghai to run the Guanhai Evening News, Meifeng lived in Wanyi Lane, while Meili lived separately at No. 601 Lafayette Road. Recently, Qi became cold and neglectful towards Meili, causing her to feel resentful. This spring, Meili hired lawyers Li Zuyu and Wu Youyuan to file a criminal lawsuit with the Second Special District District Court, accusing Qi of immorality and abandonment. After the court held a hearing, it acquitted Qi. Zhang was not satisfied and appealed to the Third Branch of the High Court, which acquitted Qi on the abandonment charge and dismissed the remaining charges. Now, Qi has hired lawyers Sun Yuan and Xu Zuyan to sue Zhang Meili in the Civil Division of the Second Special Court, alleging that she illegally detained and beat him and forced him to write a note, etc., requesting to sever family ties with Zhang. He cited Zhang Xianda and Liu Zhenfu, the doorman of Wanyi Lane, as witnesses. The court issued a summons based on the complaint. Zhang Meili still hired lawyers Li and Wu to defend her and filed a countersuit seeking reimbursement of living expenses for her children, etc. The afternoon before last, Judge Qu Z onceze held a further hearing in Civil Division Three. First, witness Liu Zhenfu testified that he had seen the plaintiff return home at 11 PM on January 2nd, with his clothes disheveled, bald-headed, and barefoot. I asked his servant to open the door for him. I don't know anything else. The plaintiff Qi Rengxi claimed that from December 31st of last year to January 2nd of this year, he was confined by Zhang Meili in her house on Lafayette Road for two days and two nights, with the front and back doors locked. On the night of the 2nd, I escaped by climbing from the window to the iron gate. Because my clothes were locked up, I wore an old robe, went home bald-headed and barefoot. I was beaten once at home, which Zhang Xianda saw, and once at her third sister Zhang Meiling's house on Laobazi Road. Her third sister also helped beat me and forced me to write a note about the money. No one saw it. I also had to write that he was the one who ran the Guanhai Evening News and took away important documents from the Guanhai Evening News. Witness Zhang Xianda runs a pharmacy. Her third sister, Zhang Meiling, is a doctor. They have an affair and are unwilling to testify in court, etc. When Zhang Meili was questioned, she detailed how she went to Tianjin in May of the 15th year of the Republic to visit her sick sister and was induced to live with him until he abandoned her now. The Guanhai Evening News was founded in Shanghai under the orders of people in the government for the sake of her husband's face, so it was outwardly said that he was running it, etc. Her agent, lawyer Li, briefly stated the intent of the countersuit and asked for legal aid. The court stated that although the main lawsuit was clear, there was still the issue of the counterclaim and legal aid, and adjourned the hearing until the aid issue had been investigated and adjudicated before proceeding with the hearing.

The Bandit Tianfu 106

Confesses to Three Kidnappings

Leading to the Arrest of Many More Bandits

Gu A'ming Vigorously Denies Being Falsely Implicated

The Zha Gate Police Station recently arrested the bandits Chen A'bing and Chen Renshou, etc., who robbed a family's property on Chengdu Road. According to their confession, there was still an accomplice named Tianfu hiding somewhere. Detective Shao Jingfan and others went to the vicinity of Deyu Lane on Guangxi Road and captured Tianfu. The bandit took the opportunity to snatch a handgun and shot Detective Shao, who was shot dead on the spot by Chinese Police Officer No. 109. This has already been reported in previous newspapers. It is now known that Chen Renshou has confessed to three kidnapping cases in previous years. He stated that the first time, he kidnapped a bank employee on Guizhou Road. However, because the hostage resisted strongly, he shot and killed the hostage on the spot. The second time, it was near the small vegetable market on Tiema Road (i.e., North Henan Road). The person kidnapped was also a banker named Lou Ken zai. However, he was only taken to Tongfu Road before being snatched away by another kidnapping gang. He received over 800 yuan in compensation from that gang. The third time, he kidnapped a Shi surname on Wu Ma Road. After two weeks, the family prepared money and redeemed him at the Jue Lu Hotel. He received 2,600 yuan. Gu A'ming was involved in all three cases except for the Guizhou Road case and said that Gu is currently hiding at No. 241 Fuzhou Road. Chinese and Western detectives then went to the address to arrest him the day before last. Gu was in the room with Hua Darong, so they were arrested together. A license plate No. 1915 was also found and taken back to the police station. It was found that Hua had also committed other crimes and was wanted by the police station. The owner of the license plate had fled recently due to a misappropriation case. Furthermore, according to Gu A'ming's confession, there were several accomplices. Chinese and Western detectives then went to Xizang Road to investigate, but only captured Fang Xiaomao. They then searched a room in the Far East Hotel for firearms based on Gu's confession, but found nothing. Zhao Jinsheng and Tang Weizhi, who were in the room, were arrested. Before long, Wang Mao'er visited Fang and was also arrested by the detectives stationed there and taken to the police station. Yesterday morning, they were all escorted to the First Special District District Court. Judge Wu Tingqi conducted the preliminary hearing. The police station also escorted Chen Renshou to the court for cross-examination. First, the police station's lawyer, Wang Yaotang, stated the circumstances of the case and requested that Chen Renshou and Gu A'ming be questioned about the kidnapping case and then adjourned so that the police station could continue to investigate. Judge Wu then questioned Chen Renshou, who confessed to the three kidnapping cases one by one, saying that Gu A'ming had arranged both the Tiema Road and Wu Ma Road Qinghefang cases and that the guns were also issued by Gu, etc. However, Gu absolutely denied it, claiming that he had helped the police station solve major cases such as the robbery of the Four Lines Preparation Warehouse in the past, which had caused the resentment of those people, and that they were now falsely implicating him in an attempt to retaliate. He hired lawyer Wu Linkun to defend him. Lawyer Wu then requested that the judge review the files of the various cases that Gu had helped solve in the past, which would prove that Gu had not committed any crimes. Judge Wu then ordered Gu A'ming and others to be remanded in custody and adjourned the hearing.

The Shishi Xinbao Labor Strike Yesterday's Report 107

The labor strike at the Shishi Xinbao has been going on for nearly a month and has not yet been resolved. Yesterday, Mr. Ge Hecai and Mr. Feng Jifang of the Shanghai Municipal Industrial Workers' Association intervened in the mediation because the strike at the newspaper was prolonged and unresolved, which would be detrimental to social order. The labor side's attitude was still to restore the situation before April 2nd as a prerequisite, and all other matters could be discussed at leisure. The management side's attitude was tough and remained the same as before, so the mediation failed again. The labor side's petition to the administrative authorities and the letters of condolence from various sectors are recorded below:

Another Petition to the Social Affairs Bureau The petition is regarding the Shishi Xinbao's management's destruction of the labor movement and the dismissal of a large number of workers without cause, requesting a swift and severe halt to the matter. The union has reported on the 2nd of this month, the authorities of Shishi Xinbao, on the pretext of the "Da Wanbao Incident," closing the factory and expelling all the workers, etc. However, since the incident, almost a month has passed. Although the Bureau and various groups have mediated, the newspaper management has relied on its fearlessness and ignored them, resulting in a prolonged unresolved situation. The union's unemployed workers have been displaced and suffered the pain of unemployment in the aftermath of this war. The management, on the other hand, has used deceitful means to sophistically argue, fooling the authorities above and deceiving the society below, not hesitating to expose the ferocious face of a civilized capitalist. Taking advantage of the increased number of unemployed workers in the society, the management disregarded social order and security and dismissed a large number of workers in order to achieve its aim of destroying the labor movement and intensifying exploitation. The union, based on the principle of labor-management cooperation, has always been patient in order to seek a peaceful solution. We respectfully request that the Bureau swiftly mediate in order to achieve the goal of returning to work as soon as possible.

The Publishing Industry Union Resigns from Mediation The Shanghai Municipal Publishing Industry Workers' Union Organizing Committee sent a letter to the newspaper industry union, resigning from the mediation. The letter reads: (Omitted above) The labor dispute in your union has been unresolved for a long time. Our union, not considering our own limitations, has engaged in mediation. Yesterday, we held discussions with the management representatives Xiong Shaohao and Ren Jinpin, etc., but they were unable to agree to the return to work and their attitude was resolute. We can only politely decline. We hope that your union will fight to the end and our union will be your support (omitted below).

The Silk Reeling Industry Union Sends Condolences The Shanghai Fourth District Silk Reeling Industry Workers' Union sent a letter of condolence, which reads: (Omitted above) Recently, we read in the newspapers that the Shishi Xinbao management, in this time of national crisis and hardship for the people, dared to use coercive tactics to destroy the organization of the labor union and even coerce the workers to reject mediation. The measures taken by the newspaper management have caused panic in society, which is regrettable. We hope that your union will fight with the spirit of the group and with justice, without giving in. Our unions are in the same boat, how can we stand idly by? We will resolutely lead all the members of the district to be your support and make vigorous efforts to deal with the Shishi Xinbao's management, who are stubborn and unwilling to repent (omitted below).

Shishi Xinbao Sues Shishi Ribao 108

For Counterfeiting Trademarks and Defamation

Xiong Shaohao, the manager of Shishi Xinbao, recently hired a lawyer to file a lawsuit with the First Special District Court against Dong Qimeng, the manager of Shishi Ribao in Fushen Lane, Zhengjia Muqiao, for counterfeiting trademarks and defamation, etc. Yesterday afternoon, Judge Feng Shide held a hearing in Criminal Division Two. The defendant failed to appear. Chinese Police Officer No. 1281 Jin Wanyun testified that he went to Zhengjia Muqiao to serve the summons yesterday, but the newspaper had already moved to No. 34 Ximen Road, French Concession. He went to the Shishi Ribao in the French Concession to notify them, and the newspaper stamped the summons and took it away. I don't know why they didn't come today. The plaintiff's agent lawyer then stated that Shishi Xinbao had registered with the Trademark Bureau and had also registered a joint trademark, Shishi Ribao, etc., which had been approved and publicly announced, granting them exclusive rights to the trademark and prohibiting others from using it. However, recently, Shishi Ribao was discovered, which not only infringed on Shishi Xinbao's joint trademark, but also the handwriting of the three characters "Shishi Bao" in its masthead was exactly the same as Shishi Xinbao. In order to seek peace and tranquility, the plaintiff sent a letter to the newspaper, asking them to change their newspaper name and demanding a reply within three days. However, they not only did not reply but also arbitrarily defamed them in the newspaper on April 9th, making unreasonable trouble. Therefore, we are suing them. Now that the defendant has been legally summoned and failed to appear without cause, we request that they be arrested. Judge Feng ordered that the case be adjourned and Dong summoned to court again for questioning.

Zhengyi Bank's Creditors Win 109

The Shareholders are Judged to Have Unlimited Liability

The Zhengyi Bank at No. 62 Jiangxi Road declared bankruptcy on November 19th of last year, leaving behind a mountain of debt. The bank's creditor groups have filed lawsuits with the court. The relationship between the limited liability company and the unlimited liability company has been the subject of dispute between the two sides. This month, a portion of the creditor group, represented by Shen Changgeng and more than ten other firms of the Chinese General Chamber of Commerce, sued the bank's directors and supervisors Ye Hongying, Qi Yongqing, Sun Jingru, Wu Yinru, and others, totaling eleven people, for failing to settle the debts. They filed the lawsuit with the First Special District Court in Shanghai, arguing that the bank did not have a license from the Ministry of Industry and Commerce and therefore could not be considered a limited liability company. They also cited the Ministry of Industry and Commerce's letter No. 9810 of the Commerce Department on January 13th (stating that the bank's license from the Ministry of Finance was a business license and could not be the basis for the bank's status as a legal entity. Although it had applied for registration with the former Beijing Ministry of Agriculture and Commerce, it had not been approved and issued a license, and therefore could not be considered a registered company. Since the bank had not obtained the legal status of a limited liability company, it was legally required to bear unlimited liability), ordering the directors and supervisors to repay the debts. On the 25th, Judge Li Hu held court in the Eighth Division and ruled that the defendants Ye Hongying and others were jointly and severally liable for repaying the debts.

Red Lips, White Hair and Another Court Appearance 110

Sun Yunqing Accused by His Concubine

Demanding the Return of a Loan of Three Thousand Yuan

Sun Yunqing, currently residing at No. 5, Jing'an Temple Alley, Jing'an Temple Road, i.e., the owner of Qinglian Pavilion on the Fourth Avenue, is 66 years old. His concubine Jiang Cuiling, who was formerly his maid and is now 27 years old, filed a lawsuit against him in the First Special District Court for abuse. After the case was settled, Jiang sued again because Sun had borrowed 3,000 yuan of silver from her personal savings and had not returned it. Furthermore, Sun had issued a promissory note, so she commissioned lawyer Chen Bingxing to sue him in court, requesting a judgment for the return of the money. The preliminary hearing was presided over by Judge Zhou Renda, who ordered that Sun return the full amount to Jiang, with interest calculated at 8% per month. Sun, dissatisfied with the judgment, appealed to the Second Branch of the High Court. Yesterday was the date for the hearing, and both parties appeared in court. According to Sun's testimony, he took Jiang as a concubine when she was 15 years old, at which time he gave her ten yuan a month for expenses. When she was 24 years old, he gave her thirty yuan a month. Later, because they were not used to living together, she demanded one hundred yuan a month and to live separately. Although the monthly allowance was increased to fifty yuan, she still felt it was not enough, and last year she even filed a lawsuit for abuse. Fortunately, the judge saw through her intentions and did not convict him. As for the alleged 3,000 yuan, there is no basis for it at all. He doesn't even know where the promissory note came from. The judge ordered him to sign his name on another piece of paper for examination. According to Jiang Cuiling's statement, she was originally from Haimen. When she was 11 years old, she was abducted and sold to the Sun family. At 15, she was forced to become a concubine. At that time, she was young and had no way to resist. The 3,000 yuan that was borrowed was when Sun joined a hui (rotating credit association) for 5,000 yuan, and she also joined for half a share. After she received the money in the 18th year of the Republic of China, Sun borrowed it. On the day she received the money from the hui, she gave him 2,000 yuan, and the next day she paid him another 500 yuan, plus 500 yuan that had been borrowed piecemeal in the past, for a total of 3,000 yuan. At that time, he wrote a promissory note, and so on. The case is now awaiting examination of Sun Yunqing's handwriting before a date is set for a retrial.

Kidnapping Case of Wang Zilin's Family 111

The Wounded Maid Dies

On the 27th of this month, at approximately 5:00 AM, three or four kidnappers went to the home of Wang Zilin, a local resident at No. 722, Yongji Lane, Weihaiwei Road, and abducted his four-year-old son, Fu Hai. The bandits also shot and wounded Wang in the leg and the maid Li Tao (38 years old) in the waist. They then escaped in a car that was parked nearby, as reported in yesterday's newspaper. The two wounded individuals were sent to the hospital for treatment, but Li Tao died from her severe injuries at 12:00 AM that night. The Xinzha Police Station ordered detectives to investigate. The body was taken to the autopsy room on Fielun Road. Yesterday morning, Prosecutor Guo Wei of the First Special District Court arrived at the autopsy room to examine the body. He sat in the official position and questioned Yu Lianquan, who stated that he and Wang Zilin were living together. At the time, Yu saw two bandits enter. One bandit snatched the child, and the other bandit guarded Yu and several others. Li Tao tried to leave, but was shot three or four times by the bandit, all hitting vital points, and so on. After obtaining the statement, Guo ordered an autopsy, which confirmed that Li Tao died from gunshot wounds inflicted by bandits. The body was released to Lian Runsheng to be prepared for burial. The police station is strictly pursuing the arrest of the fleeing bandits to bring them to justice.

Record of the Dongting Dongshan Native Association 112

The Dongting Dongshan Native Association in Shanghai held a temporary general meeting of all members the day before yesterday at 2:00 PM. Over a hundred people attended, including Qi Qisun, Wang Yizhai, and others. Zhu Xianhuai chaired the meeting, and Jiang Zhixiang recorded the minutes. The meeting began as usual. First, Chairman Zhu reported on the purpose of the meeting. Then, the secretary read the revised constitution, which was revised item by item by the committee members and voted on by the public. It was passed. Next, the issue of security in the native place was discussed. Chairman Zhu reported that bandits and robbers were rampant in Taihu Lake, and kidnapping cases were heard of daily. Residents could not sleep peacefully. He asked the public to discuss how to protect themselves. It was resolved to expand the local defense groups. Due to insufficient funds, the committee members were tasked with soliciting donations from fellow villagers in Shanghai to assist. Next, the case of soliciting members was discussed. It was decided that existing members would persuade fellow villagers in Shanghai to join as soon as possible, and a solicitation committee would be organized to actively promote membership. Finally, the issue of transportation in the native place was discussed. Xi Qisun, the general manager of Yufeng Shipping Company, reported on the spot that since the Shanghai War, bandits had been rampant in Taihu Lake, intercepting and robbing along the way, making travelers uneasy and disrupting transportation. It was difficult for fellow villagers to travel to and from Shanghai. He had built two new large gasoline boats that would travel daily between Suzhou and the native place, with special daily routes and discounted fares to show preferential treatment. Once they were completed and launched, the routes would be opened, he said. The public appreciated Xi's enthusiasm for the public welfare of his fellow villagers and the convenience of transportation, and they stood up to express their gratitude. The meeting adjourned after the discussions.

Zhang Yiru Crushed to Death by a Car 113

Anhui Native Association Provides Assistance

Zhang Yiru, from Anhui Province, was formerly a guiding committee member of the Fengyang County Party Headquarters. Last month, he came to Shanghai on official business to negotiate important matters. He stayed at the Wan Chun Gong business firm on the Fourth Avenue. On the 10th of this month, he was injured by a British public bus and sent to the hospital for treatment, but he died. His family member, Zhang Lanjie, received a telegram and rushed to Shanghai to handle the funeral arrangements. The body has been collected by the charity hall. Because the family is unfamiliar with the area and has no relatives, they specially requested assistance from the Anhui Native Association. In addition to sending a letter to the General Inspectorate of the Police, requesting that a public prosecution be initiated, and to the British Public Bus Company, requesting compensation for the loss of life, the association also hired lawyer Li Ming to file a lawsuit on their behalf.

Car Engulfed in Flames 114

The Chauffeur Was Also Burned

The Huasi Ge Factory at a certain number on Linping Road, Yangshupu, was established years ago by Chen Rufeng from Ningbo and has a thriving business. Chen owns a sedan-style car, license number 12526, which he uses for transportation, driven by Zhang Yuanhua, a 26-year-old chauffeur from Tongzhou. Yesterday morning, at around 11:00 AM, Zhang intended to drive the car to Nanjing Road to pick up his mistress, but when he reached the entrance of the Huifeng Bank branch on Huade Road, the car's engine suddenly caught fire, emitting thick smoke. French Police Station 115

French police detectives Jiang Changwen, Wang Rusong, Mao Jinsheng, and Bao detective Wang Maonan, on the day before yesterday at noon, busted a den for injecting morphine at No. 15, Deshan Lane, Fada Road. They arrested the owner, Ding Changsheng, and 14 male and female customers, including Tao Peilin, Yang Shoushi, Wang Fugen, Tang Enyu, Wang Fubao, Zhu Kun, Guo Yishan, Li Gui, Cheng Songqing, Han Yongda, Sun Wenyuan, Xin Delin, and Li Deming. Extortion Letter Sent by a Relative of a Relative 116

Zhu Weixin's Wife Recognizes the Sender

Yang Guisheng Resorts to Extortion Due to Unemployment

Zhu Weixin, the owner of Yu Kang Southern Goods Store located outside the Dadongmen gate in Nanshi, is a local resident. Due to his prosperous business, he has accumulated some savings. His family lives at No. 115, Gaoxiangtou Street, Xiaonanmen. Since last year, Zhu has repeatedly received threatening letters, which he ignored. On the 25th of this month, he received another such letter. Upon opening it, he found that it was signed "Yi Zhi Mei" (a chivalrous thief from the Qing Dynasty), stating that due to urgent needs, he was borrowing 500 yuan from Zhu. He requested that the money be wrapped in old newspaper and placed in a trash can at the entrance of a certain alley on Sangyuan Street at around 7:00 PM on the 27th, without fail. If Zhu did not comply, he would resort to drastic measures. He cited the example of Zhao Tieqiao, the former director-general of the China Merchants Steam Navigation Company, who, despite having great power, ignored the threatening letter and ended up taking "hygiene pills" (committing suicide). The letter urged Zhu not to make the same mistake. Zhu immediately reported the matter to the police at the Third Precinct of the First District. At around 7:00 PM the day before yesterday, the police first wrapped some old paper and placed it in a trash can at the entrance of a small alley on Sangyuan Street. At around 8:00 PM, a man came along, reached into the trash can, and took the paper package. The police officers, who were lying in wait around, rushed up and arrested him. During the preliminary interrogation by the precinct chief, the man confessed that his name was Yang Guisheng, 29 years old, from Huzhou. He used to be in the southern goods business, but he had been unemployed for a long time and was having financial difficulties, so he resorted to this measure. He begged for leniency. The police then sent for Zhu's wife to identify the suspect. She recognized the extortionist as a relative of Yan Zongtang, who lived at No. 96, Wanjuma Tou. They were previously acquainted, which came as a great shock. The police, regarding the matter as an extortion attempt, immediately prepared a report and submitted it to the Shanghai Municipal Police Bureau for investigation.

General Meeting of Taoyuan Fang Tenants 117

The tenants of Taoyuan Fang on Qipu Road, Hongkou, held a general meeting the day before yesterday at the Heshan Native Association in the fang. Over a hundred people attended. Feng Biao chaired the meeting. After the report was given, the discussion began, and the following cases were resolved: (1) Regarding the rent payment method for this fang: (Resolution) (A) Follow the resolution of the Shanghai Citizens' United Conference. The tenants of this fang are exempt from rent for three months. (B) Refer to the method of Junyi Lane on Ai'erjin Road, and from now on, calculate the rent at 80% of the original amount. Qipu Road was in contact with the two armies during the war, as evidenced by the records in the Shanghai newspapers of that time. Moreover, the Junyi Lane police station never lost its police power, whereas this fang did. Judging from the facts, the dangerous situation in this fang at that time was even worse. (C) According to the law of nature, rights and obligations are relative. Property owners in Shanghai do their best to ensure the safety and interests of residents. However, the facilities in this fang are inferior to others. For example, iron gates are not installed, resulting in easy access for thieves, and thefts are frequent. The tap water is damaged, the front and back doors are sometimes ineffective and cannot be closed, and there are leaks, etc. The landlord has always ignored these issues. From now on, the landlord should be requested to earnestly improve the aforementioned deficiencies and facilities to comply with the law and ensure the peace of the residents. (D) There is only one watchman, who only patrols the lane during the day. By dusk, he is gone. This is equivalent to having no watchman at all. From now on, the landlord should be requested to hire gatekeepers at the entrances of the east and west main lanes to control the entry and exit of residents late at night and to be responsible for opening and closing the gates. The executive committee should first send a letter to the landlord, arguing the case on the basis of reason. Until the negotiations are resolved, all rent payments will be temporarily suspended. (2) It was found that during the war, the Shanghai Municipal Council did not send patrols to patrol the streets of this fang, and the safety of the residents was completely disregarded. There have been multiple cases of theft and arson by plainclothes agents in this fang. (Resolution) Send a letter to the Chinese Ratepayers' Association, requesting them to ask the Shanghai Municipal Council to exempt the spring municipal general donation (i.e., patrol donation) to provide relief. Before the issue of donation payment is resolved, if the Shanghai Municipal Council sends someone to collect the donation, the summer donation should be paid, but the spring donation should be unanimously refused to ensure uniformity. (If the spring donation has already been paid, it should be deducted from the summer donation.) (3) Elect seven executive committee members. (The elected members) Qian Changcui, Li Zhuting, Feng Biao, Zhao Yaoting, Liu Wenwu, Xu Muxian, Cao Zhuqing (Remaining cases omitted)

Free Talk

Random Talk About the 19th Route Army 138

— Pillow Moon

Since the Sino-Japanese War broke out in Shanghai, the prestige of the 19th Route Army has been known almost all over the world. Previously, while serving in Nanxiang, that place was the garrison of the 78th Division of the 19th Route Army. The division headquarters was located there. At that time, Nanxiang Station was crowded with officials. The division commander, Qu Shounian, the deputy division commander, Tan Qixiu, the chief of staff, Li Kuo, and other officers would often sit in the station master's office for a while. Occasionally, when discussing national affairs with people, they always regarded the fall of the Northeast as a disgrace to the entire nation. They especially considered the inability to recover the lost territory as a great regret. When the situation in Shanghai became tense, if asked whether there would be a war, they would say, "If the government does not want our army to resist foreign invaders, we will have no choice but to join the volunteer army ourselves." Their anger was evident in their words, showing that the army's determination to resist invasion had been around for a long time. Shedding iron blood in Shanghai, it is thought that the soldiers of the 19th Route Army have had their wish fulfilled, and they must regard it as the best thing a man can do.

New Weapons 139

— Tang Jiayu

Mr. Zhou Renjie, a Cantonese, is the son of Zhou Laoyi, a charitable philanthropist in Macau. He is intelligent and creative and has studied physics and chemistry for many years. He studied in Germany and France, specializing in machinery. Recently, seeing that the country's situation is critical and that without sophisticated weapons, it is impossible to resist strong enemies and seek survival, he used his skills to invent three types of military weapons. One is the Tyrant Machine, the second is the Wind and Fire Thunder, and the third is the Electric Shock Gun. The Tyrant Machine does not need fuel, nor does it need a driver. It is propelled entirely by the automatic machine inside the machine. It can fly high or travel far. When flying, it collides with airplanes, airships, or balloons. When traveling on land, it collides with tanks and armored vehicles. When traveling on water, it collides with warships. Once hit, the explosive power is so great that it is indestructible. Even if it misses, it can emit strong electric fire to burn it. The Wind and Fire Thunder contains explosives, submunitions, and molten steel agents. The explosive power is greater than any bomb. The Electric Shock Gun is shaped like an ink pen. The content is a pseudo-electric power propulsion mechanism. Its power is more than twice that of a revolver. All three types have been tested on a small scale by military agencies. The results were extremely effective. The drawings were previously presented to the National Government and received praise. Mr. Zhou, together with Li Jingtang, the brigade commander of the Cantonese Army, came to Hong Kong from Macau last month and plans to take a boat to Beijing within days to engage in manufacturing.

Sparrow Meetings in the Countryside 140

— Jing Mengdie

The name of the meeting is "Sparrow," but it is not like the gambling dens in Shanghai. It refers to people who are like birds. Sparrows are small birds that like to eat millet. They often fly to farmyards and threshing grounds to peck freely. When they are full, they fly away without asking who the owner is. The name of this meeting is both figurative and indicative. After the outbreak of the Shanghai War, the eastern countryside of Danyi was alarmed.

Fortunately, it was spared from the ravages of war. However, the indirect impact was that financial stagnation and the decline of all industries led to a desperate situation regarding the people's food. Therefore, this unprecedented "Sparrow Meeting" arose. First, there was Qing Mianhu among the villagers, who was well-off and generous with a chivalrous spirit. Although the name was Yunyun, he was not a character from the Baishuitan. He pitied the many poor households who had no food and stepped forward to declare to the local authorities that if relief measures were not devised, people would seize food from the wealthy, and the people would become like sparrows. He asked to start with himself. Poor households responded enthusiastically, and the rich were alarmed and willing to lend grain to others. Some vulgar people closed their doors and defended themselves. The "sparrow people" gathered and came, emptying their possessions. Some carried it on their shoulders or in buckets, while others carried it in their clothes bags. They looked at each other on the road and went away leaping for joy. The hoarders cried bitterly because the lost rice was the surplus that they usually endured hunger to save, never thinking that it would be used to encourage theft. However, looking at the market, the drinkers, gamblers, and opium addicts were even more delighted to compete. Alas!

Qinglai Hall Amidst the Flames of War 141

— Zheng Yimei

Qingyun Road suffered heavy losses in the Shanghai War, and unfortunately, my humble abode was located there. My home and that of the famous painter Xu Chengbai were neighbors. After the burning and looting, there was nothing left. Then Chengbai's Qinglai Hall must also have been lost in the flames of war. When we were neighbors, we often visited each other. He did not abandon me and mistakenly regarded me as a connoisseur of painting. He spoke eloquently about the principles of painting and showed me several of his fine works, allowing me to comment on them. As far as I remember, the most exquisite and wonderful were the figure paintings. Imitating the late-year brushwork of Le Min, a beautiful woman stood with her hands clasped, with a horizontal branch of crimson plum attached above, having an air of not eating human food. The landscapes seemed to be made by Song and Yuan people. The Cloud Gorge and Long Pine Map was extremely meticulous. According to him, it took ten days to complete. It was truly a masterpiece. A small branch of plum blossoms, with only a few strokes, was elegant and unrestrained, full of charm. It was Zhao Zigu's hooking and dyeing method. Wu Chang said that plum blossoms should not be too realistic, as they would lose their refinement; they should not be too unreal, as they would lose their depiction. This painting was an image that was not like an image and an arrival that was not like an arrival. This was a good thing. Chengbai was quite proud of his work. If his works were indeed burned in this incident, then Chengbai's sorrow would be unbearable. Surviving amidst the flames of war, there has been no news. My startled soul has just settled, and I suddenly remember my old friend. I hereby write this as a memorial, and I wish the master of Qinglai Hall is well and the things in Qinglai Hall are well. That is my earnest prayer.

A Record of Bivouacking Together (38) 143

— Master of Seeking Happiness Studio

Chapter 5: Ungratefulness Leads to Estrangement, Misfortune Meets a Haughty Guest's Anger; Deep Affection Settles a Plan, It's Hardest to Bear a Beauty's Kindness

An Yutian nodded and followed Liang Xiaoyun straight into her bedroom. Such a secluded and beautiful fairyland-like place, ordinary bumpkins and unrefined men could not easily step into. An Yutian had also entered here before to admire it. An exquisite Western-style copper bed was layered with fragrant quilts and brocade blankets, embroidered pillows and velvet rugs, still so gorgeous. A room full of Western-style wooden furniture in cream color, whether it was a dressing table, mirror cabinet, jade table, or silver screen, all had artistic patterns and harmonious colors. Furthermore, the walls were lined with pink Indian satin. At this time, there was not enough light in the room, and several Beijing silk-faced palace lantern-style electric lights were turned on, illuminating it with golden brilliance, making it even more radiant. Various elements merged together, creating a kind of dazzling light, charming color, and intoxicating fragrance, gathering into another kind of unbelievable and wonderfully indescribable magic power. It could make any male who stepped in have a strange feeling of entering a labyrinth, until his soul dissipated and his bones turned to dust, even wanting to stay here until death. An Yutian was very favored today, revisiting this sacred place. As soon as he reached the door, his worries and pains were blocked outside by the door gods, not allowed to come in and disturb him. And there was another god of joy leading him, as if he had arrived in another world of bliss. He was already somewhat ethereal, no longer aware of all the sufferings of the human world. Liang Xiaoyun lay weakly and lazily on the copper bed, pointing to a bright and dazzling lamp in the middle of the bed and saying to An Yutian, "Although I don't want to get addicted to this and be controlled by it in the long run, I also like to light this lamp and occasionally take a few puffs to relieve boredom. Especially when good friends come, sitting knee-to-knee facing the lamp, we can add a lot of interest to our heart-to-heart talks. You haven't been in good spirits these past two days, why don't you lie down and take a puff?" An Yutian, unable to control himself, could not refuse. Although he also quickly obeyed and lay down, he still shook his head and said, "I'm sorry. I, this poor student, am no longer worthy of such enjoyment. Even this place of yours seems unworthy of me to step into again. Today I am here specifically to say goodbye to you. In the future, not only should we distance ourselves in terms of actions, but even that bit of friendship should also be broken off from now on. This is limited by each person's divinely ordained circumstances, and there is no way to avoid it." As he spoke, he could not help but feel sad, and his eyes gradually became moist. Liang Xiaoyun, however, smiled indifferently and said, "Oh dear. You don't even want me, this friend, anymore? But I want to ask you, what do you plan to do by yourself?" As she spoke, she skillfully prepared a puff of smoke and handed it to An Yutian, who took it in one breath.

Talks

Zheng Xiaoxu's Political Views 144

— Gou

Yesterday, a friend returned from Beiping and heard that Zheng Xiaoxu recently expressed his political views to a group of foxes and dogs. Because there were still a few people among the party members whose conscience had not been completely lost, they expressed dissatisfaction that the measures of the puppet government were completely devoid of freedom. Zheng Xiaoxu therefore expressed these political views. I heard that the most important principles and famous words were the following:

"In the past, Zhang Xun's restoration failed because his idea of rights was too developed. I now absolutely do not advocate rights, etc."

I think this sentence is very wonderful and philosophical. I have to discuss his political views briefly. The elements of establishing a country are originally based on rights. Therefore, the establishment of a country must be based on land, people, and sovereignty as the main conditions. Even those who have never studied political science mostly know this. Now that Zheng Xiaoxu "does not advocate rights," then what is left of the so-called "Manchukuo"?

I can indeed forgive Zheng Xiaoxu's difficulties and can elaborate on his meaning of "not advocating rights."

In Zheng Xiaoxu's view, I only need to restore the dynasty, I only need a place to kowtow, so the name is acceptable, a puppet is also acceptable, there is no need to insist on actual benefits. This meaning, on the surface, seems very philosophical, but his meaning is completely wrong, completely absurd.

Assuming he were truly philosophical, there would be no need to restore the dynasty. As long as political power is in hand, enlightened autocracy is acceptable, and a republican system is also acceptable. Why must he restore the dynasty? Assuming he restores a dynasty but "does not advocate rights," it is even easier to discuss. Just like when the former Emperor Xuantong was in Tianjin, others did not recognize Xuantong, but you still regarded him as Xuantong. Others did not regard him as the emperor, but you still regarded him as the emperor, going to court every day, kowtowing three times and nine times. The so-called "changing the reign title behind closed doors" restores your personal dynasty. That is also a method. Or, some say this trick, the old slave has already done it habitually, and it is not satisfying enough.

I will find him another philosophical method. The former Emperor Xuantong is already a ruler of a fallen country, like a defeated general, insufficient to establish prestige. It is better to invite a few old ancestors of the Qing Dynasty to come out, such as Tiancong, Tianming, Shunzhi, Kangxi, Yongzheng, Qianlong, Daoguang, Jiaqing, and other old emperors' ancestral tablets, and go to court every day. It would be more respectable and meaningful than going to court with Xuantong. If you say it is still not refreshing, it is not philosophical,

I will find him a more philosophical method. Zheng Xiaoxu, although he has no conscience at all, is still a descendant of the Yellow Emperor. It is better to simply invite the divine images of emperors of past dynasties, such as the Yellow Emperor, Yao, Shun, Yu, Tang, Wen, Wu, Cheng, Kang, as well as Qin, Han, Jin, Tang, Song, Ming, etc. These are genuine, truly old emperors. Go to court every day to kowtow three times and nine times. That is not impossible. Why must he temporarily perform the dream of restoration in the Northeast in the hands of the Japanese?

If it is said that the ancestors of the past are dead, but how can Xuantong, a walking corpse, be considered alive? If it is said that the ancestors of the past are empty, then is your "restoration that does not advocate rights" not empty? May I ask, both being empty and both being puppets, why must this stage be collapsed in the hands of the Japanese?

Therefore, I believe that Zheng Xiaoxu's restoration of "not advocating rights" is truly living in a drunken dream.

Science

An Engine That Doesn't Use a Boiler 146

— Translated by Zuo Qi

A new type of engine, powerful enough to break the 300-year-old method of power generation, will soon be offered to the British industrial world for trial, and its effectiveness will be observed. This new engine does not use a boiler or condenser and uses water instead of steam.

It is smaller in size than ordinary steam engines, but its power is greater, and there is no risk of explosion. The inventor is British engineer J.F.J. Malone. Mr. Malone has been researching this water engine (also called a water machine) for many years and has only recently achieved success.

Although this water engine and the steam engine that has been used for a long time both use water as a source of power, the steam engine must first turn the water into steam before it can perform any action. The water used in Malone's engine, however, remains in a liquid state even under pressure of several tons per square inch.

Malone has invented a novel heat exchanger, and it also has other advantages as follows: (1) Only a small amount of water is sufficient, so the volume of the engine can be reduced, taking up less space, making it especially convenient to install in places with a shortage of water; (2) It consumes less heat than other types of engines, and its outer shell remains cool; (3) The sound produced during operation and speed changes is quieter than that of traditional engines; (4) The parts are simpler and less prone to damage, requiring inspection only once every four years; (5) There is no need to wash the boiler frequently, no need for a water tester, and no risk of low water or sweat; (6) The management system is simpler than that of a steam engine; (7) There is no need for a venting device, as the water in the machine can be used for a long time without replacement; (8) All bearings remain cool and are self-lubricated by the water inside the machine.

Before the widespread use of electric motors, the hot air engine used in scientific laboratories was most similar to this water machine in its operating method. This water machine should use two water cylinders, each with a piston connected to the same shaft, with water moving back and forth between the two cylinders. One of the cylinders, which the inventor calls the "Thermodynamic Pile," has one end heated by the hot gas of a furnace to 900 degrees Fahrenheit, and the other end is continuously cooled by cold water or cold air to about 70 degrees Fahrenheit. The water in the cylinder circulates continuously in a set of concentric tubes, alternately being heated and cooled. These hot and cold water layers pass in opposite directions through adjacent layers at the bottom of the thermal pile, which are no more than one-hundredth of an inch thick. By this method, the heat from the furnace's hot gas can be transferred to the water extremely quickly, making it easy for the engine to run 250 times per minute.

When the water in the heat pile is heated, the pressure increases greatly, pushing part of the water into the second water cylinder, which in turn pushes the piston out, transmitting power to the machine parts. Afterward, all the water in the heat pile cools down, and the piston in the second water cylinder retracts as the pressure decreases. Thus, by using liquid instead of steam, a huge pressure change can be obtained with a smaller temperature change.

The inventor, Malone, claims: "A water engine locomotive can generate the same power as a superior steam locomotive with half the coal consumption."

Malone predicts that his new engine will be used in ships, trains, power plants, and other devices that use steam engines. This engine is especially suitable for remote areas with shortages of water and coal.

This article is translated from the American "Science News Letter" magazine.

East, West, South, North

Daily Gleanings 147

— Ji Yun

A guest familiar with the situation in Japan,

I met him at the hotel the day before yesterday. What he talked about was quite valuable to record, so I wrote it down on the left:

Since the outbreak of this war, a type of "map bread" has become popular in Japanese markets. They imprint military maps on soft, clean bread, one of the three northeastern provinces and one of Shanghai. Mountains, rivers, and major transportation routes are all clearly listed and easily visible. From this, we can see their ambition to invade is undeniable. People are rushing to buy this kind of bread to reward the soldiers on the front lines. Hundreds of boxes of this map bread have been shipped to the Hongkou Huishan Wharf. Also, when they march at night, they often have a kind of phosphorous map, which is similar to a luminous watch. In the dark, it can emit a faint green light to indicate the terrain and all the key passes. All senior military officers carry one with them. It is said that this kind of military supply was invented by the Germans during the European War, and the Japanese are just imitating it.

The remains of soldiers are mostly packed in bags and transported back to Japan. It is said that a certain military officer, because there were too many corpses and it was cumbersome to transport them back, suggested boiling the corpses into oil to be used as a raw material for smoke bombs. What a brutal thing that is! I don't know if it will become a reality or not.

Alas!

Tomorrow 148

— Xin Xiu

"Tomorrow, and tomorrow, and tomorrow, how many tomorrows there are! If I wait for tomorrow in my life, everything will be delayed." This song of "Tomorrow" has the same meaning as the Western proverb "What must be done today, do not leave until tomorrow." They are both sarcastic admonitions to people that whatever they think should be done, they should do it "decisively" and never put it off from today to tomorrow.

However, the two words "tomorrow" have almost become a cliché for Chinese people. Not only do ordinary adults and gentlemen only care about doing things as they please, regardless of whether "today" goes wrong, there is "tomorrow," and if tomorrow goes wrong, there is still "tomorrow," even the students who are studying hard and "racing against time" are like this. They get up late today, or their homework is far behind others, and they always use "I'll get up earlier tomorrow, I'll work harder tomorrow" to comfort and excuse themselves. They have forgotten the famous saying "My life has limits"! Alas, tomorrow, and tomorrow, how much precious time is wasted, and how many major events are delayed. What is written below is proof of a fact. Mr. S lived in ×× Lane in Zhabei. On the third day of the Shanghai Incident, when his roommates moved to the concession to take refuge, they repeatedly urged him to move as soon as possible. He also knew that he was in a dangerous area, but he was always lazy and procrastinated in everything. Even in that time of great anxiety, he still "put off from today to tomorrow" and did not take action immediately. But the ruthless artillery fire did not allow him to live to "tomorrow." With a bang, he was immediately invited to the ghost gate, and he became a victim of "tomorrow."

A Corner of Society

Leaving School 149

— Chen Rumin

When I leave school, the streets and alleys are always filled with the noisy voices of children with dirty faces and sweaty heads. They run around, doing meaningless things all day long. This is their life! No one to guide them! No one to manage them either.

It is a pity for these poor children who have dropped out of school. They have no money to study. The tall schools, they only have the fortune to look at them from outside the walls. Schools are originally places for aristocratic children, and knowledge is originally the monopoly of the bourgeoisie. Alas! Can the universalization of compulsory education ever be realized? This kind of grandstanding should be sung less!

Gentlemen in the administrative world! Please bow your heads and look at these millions of poor insects. Who has plundered their happiness and rights? They are regarded as the most humble things in the world, trampled on in this bustling market, groaning, begging, and dying.

If you believe that education can still save the country, what should be done about these out-of-school children who have no money? They are eagerly hoping that you can lead them into the school gate.

The remedy is to take a cheap and good product called Rice Essence, Milgen, a well-made domestic food. It contains a large amount of vitamins, which can replenish vital energy, strengthen the spleen and stomach, eliminate dampness and stagnation, and have remarkable effects on various intestinal and stomach diseases, as well as beriberi and edema. If soldiers can take one spoonful a day, their stomach strength will greatly increase.

Criminal Judgments:

The Police Department vs. Cha Kuisheng Opium Case (Main Text): Cha Kuisheng is sentenced to six months imprisonment for the crime of assisting in the sale of opium, and fined 300 yuan. If the fine is not paid, it will be converted to imprisonment at a rate of two yuan per day. The number of days of detention before the judgment is finalized will be counted as one day of imprisonment for every two days of detention. Opium, silver coins, copper coins, ledgers, etc. are to be confiscated according to the list.

The remaining accusations are acquitted. The attached civil lawsuit is transferred to the Civil Division of this court for trial.

Shanghai Local Court 153

Civil Judgments:

Cao Zhenqing et al. vs. Changshu Rice Industry Association Confirmation of Property Rights Case (Main Text): The real estate and buildings at No. 31 Xinxin Street, outside the Dadongmen Gate in South Shanghai, consisting of 2.79 acres of land and a six-story building, are confirmed to be the property of all members of the Temporary Maintenance Association of Changshu Rice Shipping Merchants in Shanghai, represented by the plaintiffs. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant.

Lin Baosheng vs. Cao Jinzhai Mortgage Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff's mortgage of 200 silver dollars and interest of 200 silver dollars. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant.

Li Zhongrun vs. Xu Hongsen Goods Payment Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff's goods payment of 138.48 silver dollars. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant.

Civil Instructions:

Wu Huasheng's request on behalf of Li Boshou et al. for an extension of the payment period has been noted. The request is denied. This is the instruction.

Yang Jiaben et al.'s request to collect exhibits has been noted. Bring the items to the court at 9:00 AM on May 2nd for collection. This is the instruction.

Li Xihua's request for arrest has been noted. Come to the court at 9:00 AM on May 2nd to receive the arrest warrant. This is the instruction.

Ouyang Tingjia's request for an extension of the payment period has been noted. An extension is granted for this week. Raise the funds and pay the case fee within the period, without delaying. This is the instruction.

Lu Jinpu's request for execution has been noted. The case has been ordered to be transmitted. Wait for interrogation. This is the instruction.

Chen Jingan's request for execution has been noted. The file has not been returned. The request will be considered later. This is the instruction.

Shu Zhenting's request for execution has been noted. Wait for the summons. This is the instruction.

Yu Yongzhou's continued request for execution has been noted. The case file has not yet been returned. The request will still be considered later. This is the instruction.

Lu Jinpu's request for execution has been noted. Wait for the order to summon and interrogate. This is the instruction.

Shao Wencai vs. Qiu Chen's Debt Re-examination Case: The request to summon has been noted. The case file has not yet been returned from the High Court and cannot proceed. The request should be considered later. This is the instruction.

Public Notice for Service:

Judgment: Ye Dachang Southern Goods Store vs. Zhu Fulin Bill Payment Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 289.34 silver dollars. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant. This judgment should be executed provisionally. The defendant Zhu Fulin is hereby notified.

Liu Anguo's request to collect exhibits has been noted. Come to the court on the 30th of this month to collect them. This is acceptable. This is the instruction.

Liu Jianchen reported that Liu Huang and others ran away and requested to file a case. If the wife of the petitioner, Huang, has committed adultery with others or has repeatedly run away with clothes, jewelry, silver dollars, etc., she can be sued for investigation. That is to say, if she has disappeared without a trace, there is no legal remedy. The request to file a case should not be considered. This is the instruction.

Shen Gongbao, in the debt dispute with Chen Xuekang, disagreed with the provisional execution judgment declared by this court and declared an appeal. Since the provisional execution part of this case has been declared disagreement, it should be submitted to the Jiangsu Higher Court for review. Since the request to stop the provisional execution until the appeal court is established is not in accordance with the law, the request should not be considered. This is the instruction.

Public Notice for Service:

Judgment: Zhang Yunqing vs. Feng Xiting Rent Arrears Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff 48 silver dollars. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant. This judgment should be provisionally executed for the first time. The defendant Feng Xiting is hereby notified.

Luo Chen vs. Li Xu Xiuying Mortgage Case (Main Text): The defendant shall repay the plaintiff's loan of 5,000 taels of silver. The litigation costs are to be borne by the defendant. The defendant Li Xu Xiuying is hereby notified.
